 In the Chandel district of Manipur, 18 soldiers were martyred and 11 others were injured in this attack ambushed by an army contingent
 ise sena par haal ke varshon main sabase bada hamalaa bataaya ja rahaa he
 The attack was carried out by NSCN (K) militants and was also helped by rebel groups like the UNLF
 samajha jaataa he ki ye gut china se shah praapt sanghathan united librasion front of western south asia kaa ang he
 Apart from Nagaland-based NSCN (K), United Liberation Front of Assam Independent or ULFA (I), National Democratic Front of bodoland-sonbijit or NDFB (S) of Assam and Kanglei Yawol Kunna Lup or KYKL of Manipur are all part of the new organization 
 enessien(ke) ne 4 june ko sena par hue hamale se kuch hi din pehle puraane sangharshaviram samjhaute ko tod diya tha
 According to investigators of the National Investigation Agency (NIA), RK Meighen (RK Meghen), the head of the rebel faction of Manipur, UNLF, reported that his group had been in contact with China since 2008
 usne yah bhi bataaya ki 2008 main kathmandu main usne china ke agent se mulaakaat kii thi, jiskaa code naam elex tha

 iske baad china kii khufia agency ek duusari nijee kapanni Aye Kyi Kaung Co Ltd ke jariye yuanelef ke sampark main rahi
 The meeting took place in Ruili city in western Hunan
 jaanchakartaaon ke mutabik, yahaan chini agency ne yah jaanane kii koshish kii purvottar main bhartiya sainikon or mixilon kii tainaati kaise ho rahi he

 The search engine Google today recalled the famous Indian scientist and statistician Prashant Chandra Mahalanobis on his birthday through Doodle
 aaj prashanth chandra kaa 125waan janmdin he
 He was born on 29 June 1893 in Kolkata
 aaie jaanate hai unase judi kuch baaten
 
 - prashanth ko prashanth mahalanobis dystence kaa pataa lagane ke liye sabase zyada shoharat mili, jo do data set ke bich duuri kii tulana karata he
 - Establishment of Indian Statistical Institute and Central Statistical Institute to bring synergy in statistics related activities
 - aapako bataa den, unka janmdin 'sankhyikee diwas' ke rup main manaaya jaataa he
 - In view of the contribution made by Mahalanobis in the field of Statistics, the Government announced in June 2007 as Statistics Day every year
 mahalanobis ne bhartiya sankhyikee santhaan kii sthapana 1931 main kii thi
 Know about the wizard of data - As a member of the Planning Commission, he formulated India's strategy for industrialization in the Second five-year Plan
 - graphic aadhaarit vishleshan ke jariye unhone alag-alag tabakon ke saamaajik-aarthik halaat kii tulana bhi kii
 In 1949, he was appointed as Honorary Statistical Advisor to the Government of India
 - unhen saal 1968 main padam vibhushan se nawaja gaya tha

 uparashtrapati em venkaiya naidu ek program main 29 june yani aaj ye sikaa jari karenge

 aapako bataa den, 125 rupee kaa saath 5 rupee kaa nayaa sikaa bhi jari kiya ja rahaa he

 unki shuruaati shiksha unke dada dwaara banawaye ‘brahm boij skool’ main hui

 Lord Vishnu is fasted on this day
 manyata he ki kaamada ekadshi kaa vrath karne se sabhi kashton se mukti milti he

 vrath puja se laabh-kaamada ekadshi ke din vishnu bhagwaan kii puja kii jaati he

 manyata he ki is din vrath-pujan karne se adhuri manokamanaayen vishnu bhagwaan puri karte he

 - subah snaan karke safed pavitra vastra pahanen or vishnu dev kii puja karen
 - Offer yellow marigold flowers, mango or melon, sesame, milk and peda to Vishnu Dev
 - namo bhagavate vasudevaye kaa jaap karen
 - Offer food to the temple priest and give Dakshina
